This reduction of invasive and overgrown plants, and resulting increase in native vegetation, ensures that various animal species have a home, and that the ecosystem will function efficiently, providing all nearby life with significant benefits. https://t.co/RaG3glokqC
The goats are able to eliminate vegetation threatening native plants, and thus biodiversity, without creating additional threats to the overall health of the ecosystem that other methods, like chemicals, could pose. https://t.co/a8oLnMhahL
When invasive plants take over, there is a decline in the amount and effectiveness of ecosystem services provided to wildlife and people living/working nearby.
Healthy environments rich in biodiversity provide various important ecosystem services to people and wildlife in the area, such as oxygen production, flood mitigation, erosion prevention, nutrient storage/recycling, pollution filtration, carbon dioxide reduction, and more.
By clearing invasive, nuisance, and overgrown landscaping, our goatscapers (at our Narragansett, RI Lab) will help increase plant and animal biodiversity in the area, and improve ecosystem health both above and below the ground. https://t.co/VCvZaWe1z2
